\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Manage a piecewise clothoids $ G(s) $ composed by n clothoids (not necessarily G2 or G1 connected)

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{load()}{load()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_g2lib_1_1_clothoid_list_ab9e6c0c352c3ad9a553d925fff2b24af} 
void G2lib\+::\+Clothoid\+List\+::load (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_g2lib_a7ed8321a8bada9eae2f914f6fb70a208}{istream\+\_\+type}} \&}]{stream}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_g2lib_acc8095aa40beedee44352de62f232033}{real\+\_\+type}}}]{epsi}{ = {\ttfamily 1e-\/8}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Read the clothoid list from a stream. The data is assumed to be saved as follows \begin{DoxyVerb}  # x y theta kappa
  x0 y0 theta0 kappa0
  x1 y1 theta1 kappa1
  ...
  xn yn thetan kappan
\end{DoxyVerb}

Save the clothoid list on a stream. The data is saved as follows \begin{DoxyVerb}  # x y theta kappa
  x0 y0 theta0 kappa0
  x1 y1 theta1 kappa1
  ...
  xn yn thetan kappan
\end{DoxyVerb}
